--- Commit Message ---
LU-17916 osd-ldiskfs: switch to struct folio of order 0

Prefer folio of order 0 to struct page and switch to the folio API.
Drop the page used to hold options during server mount, any kmalloc
memory can be used here.

HPE-bug-id: LUS-12384
Signed-off-by: Shaun Tancheff <shaun.tancheff@hpe.com>
Change-Id: I2d24e2ace8d84e9e6b5db764efbd2b06fb42d8a3
